Vintage Super League Season 4 Decklists
=======================================



 Posted in [Magic Online](/en/gameinfo/products/magiconline/decklists)
 on March 9, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











Below are the decklists for Vintage Super League Season 4. Watch the excitement unfold Tuesday nights at 6:00 p.m. Pacific on [twitch.tv/magic](http://www.twitch.tv/magic)!


Follow the links below to take you to each player's current decklist.


[DOWNLOAD MAGIC ONLINE](mtgo.com/SignUp)
